  295. Do pheromone products work? Perhaps, but the strongest effect is probably placebo effect.<br /><br />Zyloo Labs (PherX) indicates that these products are effective for up to four hours. As far as I can tell the only noticeable effect is darn near &#34;point blank&#34; (about one foot or less).<br /><br />Response may depend a lot on the female inhaling the pheromones. I have been conducting research and every female has indicated she likes the smell. However as far as an &#34;attractant&#34; as the product is pitched, only one female (out of about 50 test subjects) actually responded with what you'd indicate as &#34;amazing&#34; response.<br /><br />My intuition after two months of research and observing reactions is that the response is extremely variable (unpredictable), generally minor (might get an extra smile or two), and overall other factors (self confidence) will be far stronger influences.<br /><br />I like the spray version because it delivers a nice solid burst which is plenty to apply. The &#34;oil&#34; version is best used for dabbing a little behind the ears or any other location where you want precision in placing it. The applicator on the oil bottle is poorly designed and if you put your fingertip on the top of the bottle then use it like you would any cologne you will get almost nothing out of the bottle, you have to be a bit creative and aggressive with the oil bottle to get any reasonable amount out. Thus I prefer the spray bottle.
